建筑專刊

大陸銀行信託部建築大陸商場的緣起 186

上海是成爲現代中國首屈一指的大　。　　的貿易。工商業的繁盛。也在世界大都市中。占了第六位。這是大家所　　　　不過我們細細的一加考察。雖則看到上海的區域是這樣的遼闊。但是　　　　繁盛的中心地。方圓恐怕也不過只有幾里罷。試想在這點僅僅幾里方圓　　　地域。要聚集無數中外新舊的工商業。事實上是然很湧擠緊凑。難乎其難了。所以他排我擠。甚至你占我奪。那力量比較得雄厚點的。還免强可以獲得寸尺之地。那力量薄弱的。那末只得被排擯在市外了。現在有多少的大工廠大商店。因爲得不到一個中心地位。來陳列樣品。或是營業所。退而取其次。因此事業不能發展。到後來失敗。甚至虧蝕。看來眞可痛惜。那裏是他們資本不厚，人才不優，出品不良的原故呢？

成功一個繁盛的中心市區。也是絶對不能以一朝一夕。一人一力。可以做得到的。他有他的形勢和歷史。那末上海的繁盛中心。旣是這樣的陜遏。所以要想救　這個緊急的需要。就不得不想個特殊的方法了。上海大陸銀行信託部。他以服務社會的職志。和補助工商業的使命。他鏖到了這個的重大缺憾。尤其是我國落後的工商業。所感受到的痛苦。更爲深刻。所以非馬上的來解决不可。於是就有這大陸商場創辦的動議。其間經過了很久的研究和討論。就覺得選擇塲址。最爲困難。後來終以上海現代商務的情形。和將來發展的趨勢。就勘定了北臨南京路。東臨山東路。南臨九江路。西臨又新街的一方大地。爲建造商塲的塲址。至於這個地位的優越。形勢的重要。和交通的便利。的確是在上海繁盛中心地内。可算數一數二的了。他東面距離黃浦是十分接近。西面又緊接着畫錦里（山西路）日升樓（浙江路）一帶。南面從法租界來。又不遠。北面到火車站虹口去。又極方便。所以成爲一個全市的衝衢。貿易的途隘。而且面積的容量也很大。足有九畝多地。有了這個的大好區處。來建築一所偉大輝煌的商塲。是再也適合没有了。不過地主。雖是哈同洋行。但是大陸信託部早已具了遠大的計劃。已經訂好了很久的租約（三十二年）。

正在建築中之大陸大樓由基泰建築工程司設計申泰興記營造廠承造

莊俊建築師設計

公記營造廠承造

大陸信託部勘定了塲址以後。就在民國二十年春。交付上海著名建築師莊俊先生設計打樣。莊先生就參考了世界各國最新的計劃作爲標準。再補充以現代的需要。和我國的習慣。本來莊先生有了很深的經騐。就很迅速的計劃完成這個偉大建築。同時就由本埠公記營造廠以規元七十餘萬兩的造價得標承造。在同年三月十九日就行開工大吉的典禮了。本來預定是七個半月可以全部交屋。但是不幸的滬戰爆發。因而中間停頓了幾個月。後來等到恊定簽字。社會恢復了原有狀態之後。公記營造廠趕即完成他未竣的建築。到今年的國慶時候。於是這所上海破天荒的大商塲。方得與我們相見。再看興建這樣一所大厦。其間總合只需要僅短短幾個月的工夫。眞是不得不欽佩公記營造廠力量的偉大與神速

房屋大槪與

飯店弄堂之今昔

查公共租界工部局工務處。列來所發給出來的建築執照。要算建造大陸商塲爲最大。那末這商塲面積的廣大。和全厦建築的雄偉。當然在現代的上海市區内。是數一數二的。而且屋基的四面。都是臨接大路。靠南京路方面的正中部分。有高屋八層。兩旁亦都有七層。在山東路轉角處。建有巍塔。計九層。高聳入雲。也是全屋的最高峯。沿九江路的一面。都是四層。全屋係由水泥工程師繆凱伯先生的設計。築成極堅實的幹骨。所以在莊嚴雄秀之外。十分的結固。專配置上東方和上海二鋼窗公司承辦的全部鋼窗。看上去。自然是更覺得優秀美麗了。

1932.12.26

Today's Main Points of This Newspaper 1

Domestic: Japanese Soldiers' Trains on the Jin-Chao Line are Non-Stop; Koiso Going to Inspect the Rehe Border; He Chengjun Going from Hankou to Shaanxi; Righteous Army Recaptures Longwangmiao; Central Government Holds Yunnan Uprising Commemoration

Foreign: Germany, Austria, and Hungary Grant Amnesty to Political Prisoners; Pope Delivers Speech on the State of the World's Churches

Shanghai: Guangdong Committee Member Cui Guangxiu Returns to Guangdong; Zhu Jiahua and Wu Tiecheng Discuss Postal Savings Merger Methods

A Large Japanese Army Advances Towards the Jin-Chao Line 2

Reaching the Chaoyang Area, Numbering Over 100,000

Soldier Trains Non-Stop from Beining to Jinzhou

Fierce Fighting with the Volunteer Army, No Contact with Formal National Army Yet 3

Chief of Staff Koiso Rushes from Shenyang to the Rehe Border

(Beiping) Japanese troops advanced towards the Jin-Chao Line. The foremost positions were in Chaoyang Temple, where they came into contact with the righteous armies of Zhu Jiqing, Wang Yunping, Meng Zhaoyan, Li Haifeng, Ma Zidan, and others. Japanese planes flew to the Rehe border for days, dropping intimidating leaflets. Japanese armored vehicles were stationed at Chaoyang Temple Station. To guard against the righteous army, the Japanese army fired artillery at night as a show of force. On the morning of the 23rd, five trains departed from Dahu Mountain on the pseudo-Fengshan route, each carrying five to six hundred Japanese soldiers with heavy ammunition, arriving in Jinzhou without disembarking, turning onto the Jin-Zhi Road towards Yixian. Two Japanese transport trains travel daily on the Jin-Chao Line, and people are prohibited from observing when they arrive at the station. Japanese soldiers patrol back and forth with guns. On the night of the 23rd, Japanese armored vehicles fired four shots near Wanjiatun, and the sound of artillery was heard in Shanhaiguan, attacking the righteous army. The Zheng Guilin's troops in Jinxi sometimes dismantled the road at night, so the Japanese armored vehicles fired artillery as a show of force. (25th Dispatch)

Tang Yulin's Troops Firmly Defend Their Positions 4

(Beiping) Tang Yulin reported from Chengde to Beiping this morning, stating briefly that the Japanese army's attack on Rehe has indeed begun to prepare, and has been dispatching planes to reconnaissance and bomb the Rehe border, causing increasing unease among the people. The Japanese army has been fiercely fighting with the righteous armies in Kailu, Fuxin, Yixian, Zhoujiatun, and other places for days. Our army is firmly defending its positions and quietly observing the situation. As of 5 AM this morning, there has been no contact with our formal troops. The Rehe River is as peaceful as usual, etc. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Due to the urgency of the Rehe situation, Tang Yulin specially dispatched Councilor Li Xiaopeng to Beijing on the 25th to report on the recent situation on the Rehe border. (25th Dispatch)

Pseudo-National Salvation Army Opens in Chaoyang Temple 5

(Beiping) The first detachment of the National Salvation Army's special operations team, organized by Cheng Guorui in Jinzhou, departed for Chaoyang Temple on the Jin-Chao Road train on the 23rd. The entire team consisted of over a thousand soldiers, who were issued firearms and ammunition from the Shenyang Arsenal, and will advance from Chaoyang Temple to attack Beipiao. (25th Dispatch)

Koiso Hurries to the Rehe Border for Inspection 6

(Beiping) Japanese Chief of Staff Koiso departed from Shenyang on the 23rd and arrived in Jinzhou on the 24th for inspection. He then returned to Suizhong, alighting from the train and switching to a car to inspect the Rehe border. The Rehe border is crowded with Japanese troops, including the Suzuki Brigade and the Sanjian Masaru unit, about one regiment, and recently transferred a part of the Eighth Division Army, about four thousand soldiers. There are many other miscellaneous troops, all colluding with Mongolian bandits, lamas, ruffians, and local gangsters. The Japanese army in the Chaoyang area claims to have over 100,000 soldiers. (25th Dispatch)

The Japanese Create Pretext Again 7

⊙Jinzhou Former Liaoxi Times employees Ito Sekiho, Masuda Sukaji, and two Manchurians they guided were brutally murdered at the border of the Rehe River in the Zamu Linzi area on the afternoon of the 18th at 1 p.m. while investigating the urgent situation in the Rehe area. The truth of the incident is currently being investigated, and its outcome is quite important. (25th Electric Communication)

Feng Zhanhai's Troops Occupy Tongliao County Town 8

The Japanese Army in Bayan is Cut off From Retreat

(Beiping) Feng Zhanhai's unit of over ten thousand men began to clash with the stationed Japanese army in Bayan at Xiawa. Feng dispatched three thousand elite soldiers, detouring to the Bayan River, and fiercely attacked Tongliao, having already occupied Tongliao County Town. The Japanese army in Bayan, about five hundred soldiers, is cut off from retreat, and the entire army is on the verge of annihilation. (25th Dispatch)

Four Consulates in Russia Will be Restored First 9

The Rest Are Also Being Reorganized

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, there are many Chinese nationals living in Russia who are in urgent need of protection. After Ambassador Yan Huiqing's orders are announced, the consulates in Miaojie, Teluoyi, Shuangchengzi, and Duorkucike will be restored immediately, and it is also planned to reorganize the existing consulates in Dingsanganjiyan, Tashkent, Almaty, Xiemi, Chita, Bolly, Heihe, and Vladivostok.

(25th Dispatch)

Feng Zhanhai's Representative Arrives in Beijing, Appealing for Aid to the Soldiers' Hardships! 10

Straw and Saddles to Ward Off the Cold

Grass Roots and Tree Bark to Fill Their Stomachs

(Nanjing) Feng Zhanhai sent representative Xia Yunlong to Nanjing to appeal for aid from all sides. According to reports, his unit has fought over a hundred battles, large and small, with the Japanese and rebel armies. To date, there are over 80,000 men, fully equipped with artillery, infantry, and cavalry, with complete firearms and horses. Because of the lack of economic resources in the defense area, the troops have been rotated back to Rehe for replenishment since last month. Currently, 40,000 men are stationed in Kailu, Jianping, Fuxin, Suidong, Lingyuan, and other counties. The Sun and He units are engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese army in the Zhan Yu area. There are about 45,000 men remaining in Jilin, two-thirds cavalry and one-third infantry, stationed in Lalin Yushu, Wuchang, Acheng, Shulan, and other counties. They have repeatedly attacked the Japanese army, but all the soldiers have no houses to live in, and due to lack of nutrition, they are all sleeping in the open. The sentries are mostly wrapped in straw and carrying saddles to ward off the cold. Sometimes, supplies are insufficient, and they eat grass roots and tree bark to fill their stomachs. During battles, they often go three to five days without a full meal. Families of soldiers who died in battle have no means of support. There are currently over two hundred women and children following Commander Feng to seek food. Therefore, he urgently hopes that the central government and all parties will provide material assistance. Recently, the Japanese have been increasingly eager to invade Rehe. Japanese armored vehicles frequently travel to the Chaoyang Nanling area to fire artillery in provocation, and airplane bombings and bombings occur almost daily. The reason they have not yet launched an immediate attack is to first eliminate the righteous army before attempting a major offensive. (25th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The seventh division of the tenth district of Beijing City raised 6,000 yuan to aid the righteous army from the staff of various agencies, schools, workers, and friends in the district. On the 25th, it was handed over to the custodians Ge Mingxun and Yu Zhaochun to be remitted to the Beijing Shanghai Bank free of charge. (25th Dispatch)

Righteous Army Recaptures Longwangmiao 11

Japanese Army Collapses Towards Anshan-Shenyang Line

Shiyan Can Be Recovered Immediately, Japanese Army Sends Three Routes for Reinforcement 12

Japanese Army Decides to Launch General Offensive Today

(Beiping) The righteous army of Deng TieMei is fighting fiercely with the Japanese rebel army. Longwangmiao has been recaptured by our army, and the Japanese army is collapsing towards the Anshan-Fengtian line. On the 20th, our army advanced along the Dayang River towards the Japanese army at Dagushan. The enemy retreated step by step and can be captured within a day. Shiyan is surrounded by our army and can be recovered immediately. On the 20th, four Japanese planes scouted our position and landed at Baimiaozi. They were captured by our army's Li Zirong unit, the driver was executed by firing squad, the inside of the plane was dismantled, and it was temporarily stored in the rear of our army. In the Yingkou, Panshan, Gaiping, and Haicheng areas, 3,000 men from our army's Wang Quanyi, Li Zirong, Weng PinSan, and other units fought fiercely with the rebel army's Wang Dianzhong and Li Shousan units. On the morning of the 19th, the Tian Xiaohao unit fought fiercely with the rebel army's Wang Dianzhong unit for two hours on the north bank of the Liao River. The rebel army was defeated, and the Tian Xiaohao unit won a great victory, killing countless enemies and capturing many weapons. (25th Telegram)

(Beiping) The Jilin National Salvation Army Headquarters reported to Ping by telegram on the 19th that the violent Japanese dispatched a team to attack our army in Shulan on the morning of the 13th. After Wu Yicheng, the overseer of Changjiang River, greeted Jiang Ru's unit to fight back, the battle was very fierce. Our army used the terrain to its advantage, and the soldiers first used tree branches and mountain grass to make thousands of grass men, all wearing tattered clothes and hats, standing around the top of the mountain, attracting the attention of the Japanese. All the strong troops were dispersed in the important fortresses, and another elite team of more than two thousand men was selected and ambushed on the left side of the mountain, waiting for the right time to penetrate deeply and strike hard. The enemy continued to increase reinforcements, gathering more than five thousand troops, and suddenly bombarded our side. Our army waited for the enemy to chase into the mountain pass by more than half, and then the ambushing troops rose up, and the enemy retreated. We tracked down and killed the enemy in a very embarrassing situation, with countless casualties. Our army suffered eleven casualties and captured countless spoils of war. (25th Dispatch)

(Dalian) The Kurosaki unit has been surrounded by the righteous army in Xiuyan since then, and there has been no news so far. The Kwantung Army believes that the entire army has been wiped out. This morning, a carrier pigeon flew back, and it was only then that the battle situation before the 23rd was known. At that time, the unit had suffered more than half of its casualties. The Japanese army then mobilized the Iwata unit, the Iida unit, and the Kindai unit, and went to rescue from three sides. Another five planes were dispatched from Dashiqiao, carrying bombs to reconnaissance at the position and bombing the righteous army. (25th China United Press Telegram)

(Shenyang) The Kumazaki unit, which was surrounded and held in Xiuyan by the righteous army, released a carrier pigeon for help. Yesterday afternoon at 4 o'clock, it arrived at the Anshan garrison team and reported as follows: As of today, one public security team member has died in battle and three have been injured. The ○ team has not suffered any damage. At 11 a.m. on the 23rd, a plane flew over and circled the county seat. The pilot, Captain Fujita, seemed to have been injured by enemy bullets. The ○ team has no food supply, and besides pigeons, there is no other means of communication. There are not many remaining grenades. Please replenish them quickly. (25th Electric Communication Telegram)

(Shenyang) The Iwata ○ unit, which was chasing Xiuyan from Chemu City, encountered about a thousand righteous soldiers from Li Rong's unit at noon yesterday. After a fierce battle, the advance of the unit and the motorcade was blocked. They had no choice but to camp there last night. In addition, the Ueda unit, which was advancing from the Anshan side, also fought fiercely with over a thousand righteous soldiers near Guanmen Mountain, and also camped there. The general attack is scheduled to begin on the morning of the 26th. (25th Electric Communication Telegram)

North China Generals to Hold Security Conference 13

Yang Aiyuan and Sun Dianying Arrive in Beiping

(Beiping) Due to the urgency of the Rehe River situation and the importance of security in North China, North China generals plan to jointly discuss the strategy of resisting aggression and defending the territory based on the principles of the previous Political Committee meeting. Yang Aiyuan arrived in Beiping this afternoon, and Sun Dianying is scheduled to arrive in Beiping tonight. Shang Zhen and Fu Zuoyi will also come to Beiping. Song Zheyuan can arrive tomorrow to meet with Han and visit Zhang. A solution has been discussed for Feng's residence issue, and Feng's opinion is being sought. It can be resolved soon. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Dianying arrived in Beiping tonight. North China generals plan to take the opportunity to discuss ways to reduce military spending. Ma Hongkui telegraphed Ping, saying that he would come to Ping to see Zhang in a few days and then go to Ningxia to take office. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yang Aiyuan said that the results of the Third Plenary Session were very good. Wu Chaochu proposed a motion for armed resistance against Japan, which was passed in principle. The detailed plan was handed over to the Political and Legal Conference for review and implementation. Jiang summoned him several times and inquired in detail about the current situation in Shanxi Province. He passed by Ping to meet with old friends. Yan Jin is actively carrying out the plan to develop the Northwest. Regarding the plan to build the Tongpu Road, Yan advocated completing the roadbed project first and has sent personnel to investigate. Bandits in Shanxi Province have been restrained. Bao Gang and other guest troops in Qin County are still raising funds locally and have requested the government to exempt the people from bearing the burden. He will visit Zhang after seeing him and return to Shanxi in a day or two. (25th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Shang Zhen returned to Shunde on the evening of the 25th after completing his affairs in Beijing. (25th Dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang Hosts Banquet to Welcome Han Fuqu 14

(Beiping) This morning, Han Fuqu visited Jiang Bocheng and Wang Shuchang for a long time. Zhang Xueliang hosted a banquet at the Prince Shuncheng's Mansion tonight to welcome Han, inviting Jiang Bocheng, Shen Honglie, Wan Fulin, and Men Zhizhong to accompany him. After the banquet, Han met with Zhang to discuss issues such as the naval garrison in Yantai and Longkou. Wan Fulin is scheduled to host a banquet for Han Fuqu and Shen Honglie tomorrow night. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Han Fuqu visited Zhang at the Prince Shuncheng's Mansion last night with Liu Xizhong and talked for a long time. Han visited Zhu Qinglan this afternoon. (25th Dispatch)

Director of the Shandong Civil Affairs Department Inspects Longkou and Huang County 15

Spoke to Various Circles in Laiyang

(Jitong) The Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Li Shuchun, spoke to various circles in Laiyang, briefly stating that Chairman Han had no choice but to launch the Jiaodong Incident. The people suffered greatly, and the chairman was deeply ashamed. He originally wanted to come in person, but due to unforeseen circumstances, he sent Yu as his representative to first leave 400,000 catties of coarse grains and 200,000 catties of grass, as well as 600 piculs of grain, and also allocate them to relieve disaster victims, investigate the deaths of those killed, and provide condolences. At that time, the people of Laiyang requested exemption from the Ding Cao, and Li agreed to forward it to the provincial government. Early on the 24th, Li personally inspected the disaster situation in the town and various agencies, and went to Longkou in the afternoon. He has now arrived in Huang County. Li telegraphed the provincial government, stating that the Laiyang No. 9 Middle School suffered losses and requested a temporary fee of four to five thousand yuan to resume classes. (25th Dispatch)

Beijing Social Affairs Bureau Plans to Build Three Scenic Forests 16

(Nanjing) The Social Affairs Bureau plans to build three scenic forests: Jiming Temple, Lion Mountain, and Qingliang Mountain, and plant trees and build them next spring. (25th Dispatch)

Central Government Holds Yunnan Uprising Commemoration 17

Beijing City Party Headquarters Also Holds Grand Meeting

(Nanjing) The Central Party Headquarters held the 17th Anniversary Commemoration of the Yunnan Uprising on the morning of the 25th. Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Zhang Zhen, Miao Peicheng, etc., and over three hundred staff members attended. Ye Chucang presided over the meeting and performed the ceremony. Ju Zheng reported, briefly stating that in 1915, when Yuan Shikai claimed the title of Emperor, the revolutionary comrades in Yunnan first telegraphed Yuan to oppose him, and then announced independence. Yuan then cancelled the imperial system, and the Republic of China was restored, making it one of the most glorious pages in the history of the Republic of China. Later, he said that commemorating the Yunnan Uprising requires recalling this spirit and striving to resist aggression and seek national strength. (25th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Special Party Headquarters of the Central Military Academy held a commemoration of the Yunnan Uprising on the morning of the 25th. Representatives from the eighth and ninth classes of the higher education classes and all members of the military training class, more than eighteen hundred people, attended. Zhang Ji was invited to give a speech in advance. Zhang presided over the meeting, performed the ceremony, and reported on the course and significance of the Yunnan Uprising. He then said that to save the country, it is necessary to actively build the Northwest and restore the cultural spirit of thousands of years, using the national strength of the Zhou, Qin, Han, and Tang dynasties to make the Chinese nation stand forever in Asia and contend with Japanese imperialism, and further achieve the Three Principles of the People and seek national equality in the international community. Zhang gave a very detailed explanation of the Northwest issue, including the international situation, the recovery of the lost Northeast, the analysis of Chinese history and culture, the future political direction, and the essentials of national survival, which moved the audience. (25th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Beijing City Party Headquarters convened a grand meeting of representatives from all circles at 9:00 a.m. on the 25th to commemorate the Yunnan Uprising. Over two hundred representatives from the State Council, the Legislative Yuan, the Control Yuan, the Examination Yuan, various ministries, departments, the Training and Supervision Department, the Construction Committee, the Ministry of Internal Affairs, the Ministry of Justice, the Ministry of Communications, the Ministry of Finance, the Examination Committee, the municipal government, various agencies, lower-level party headquarters, mass organizations, and schools attended. Gu Zhengding presided over the meeting, reported on the course and significance of the Yunnan Uprising, shouted slogans, and adjourned the meeting. (25th Central News Agency Telegram)

Yu Xuezhong Tours Yesterday 18

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong led personnel from the civil, financial, military, police, and legal departments on a special train tour on the morning of the 25th. Yu told reporters that he inspected the troops stationed along the line, assessed the performance of officials, and visited people's concerns, and planned to pass through Dongguang, Jingxian, Yanshan, Qingyun, Cangxian, Jinghai and return to Tianjin. (25th Dispatch)

Tax Revenue Expected to Increase After Resumption of Sino-Russian Diplomatic Relations 19

(Nanjing) According to financial circles, customs revenue for September, October, and November was about the same as in the same months last year. According to statistics reported by various customs houses, customs revenue for this month is expected to increase by more than 800,000 compared to last month. After the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Russian goods are being shipped to China for sale one after another. Although enemy goods have been eliminated, there should be an improvement in the tax revenue from the import of Russian goods in the future. It is expected that national customs revenue may increase in January. (25th Dispatch)

Headquarters Establishes Henan Post-War Rehabilitation Committee 20

Organizational Regulations Promulgated

(Hankou) The Headquarters established the Henan Special Zone Post-War Rehabilitation Committee, composed of one person each from the Henan Provincial Party Headquarters, the Provincial Government, and the Pacification Headquarters, three people from the 20th Route Army Headquarters, one person from the 1st Army Headquarters, and two people from the Henan 9th District Administrative Commissioner's Office, as members. They are appointed by the Headquarters, and the Director and Deputy Director are designated. The ten organizational regulations were promulgated on the 25th. (25th Dispatch)

Mongolian Beijing Fellow Townsmen Welcome Panchen Lama and Zhangjia 21

(Nanjing) The Mongolian Beijing Fellow Townsmen Association and the Mongolian Cultural Promotion Association held a meeting at the Central Hotel on the 25th to welcome Panchen Lama and Zhangjia. Bai Yunti delivered a welcome speech, and Panchen and Zhangjia each gave a reply, all encouraging each other with national unity, saving the country, resisting aggression. (25th Dispatch)

Ministry of Railways Plans to Build Central Station 22

(Nanjing) The Central Station construction plan of the Ministry of Railways will connect the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai), Jinpu (Tianjin-Pukou), Xiangshuo (Hunan-Guangxi), and Jingyue (Beijing-Guangzhou) lines. The Central Station will be located north of the Houzaimen (Back Gate) of the Ming Palace, bounded by Houzaimen to the south, the Central Military Academy and the Lishi Society to the west, and the city walls to the northeast. There are three lines connecting various roads. (1) The connection of the Jinghu Line is stipulated to bifurcate at the Mule House place at the west end of the fork in the line, pass through Tangjiashan and Xinzhuang, and then fold south into Ziyoumen (Freedom Gate) to the Central Station. (2) The connection of the Jinpu Line is stipulated that the current capital railway ferry across the Yangtze River bifurcates near Hepingmen (Peace Gate) on the Jinghu Line, travels west of Xinzhuang, goes south, enters Ziyoumen, and reaches the Central Station. In the future, if a bridge or tunnel can be built across the river, it is planned to cross the river at Beihekou (North River Mouth) outside Shuiximen (Water West Gate), connect to the industrial area and travel east, then connect to Jingxiang and Jingyue and travel north into the city to the Central Station. (3) The connection of the Jingyue and Jingxiang lines is measured to be two lines, one line circling Zijin Mountain, meeting Jinghu, entering Ziyoumen, and the other line going north along the city wall from Yinxiang Town to the north of Zhongshanmen (Sun Yat-sen Gate) and entering the city to the Central Station. After comparison, it was decided to adopt the second line to the Central Station. If you take the road from Xuancheng to Wuhu to Beijing, then pass through another line to Hexiang Town at the Jianggu Li Village along the river, and then take the second line to the Central Station. (25th Dispatch)

Yang Hucheng Telegraphs That He Has Occupied Sidu River 23

(Nanjing) Yang Hucheng telegraphed Beijing on the 23rd that Zhao Shoushan's brigade would attack the bandits entrenched in the Sidu River area in coordination with Wang Zhiyuan's brigade and Zhang Junrong's unit. Under fierce fighting, the bandits fled to the Zhongjiawan Jingdangba area. Our army has now occupied the Sidu River. The remaining bandits seem to be fleeing to Tongjiang County in Sichuan. The vanguard has already reached Lianghekou today. (25th Dispatch)

He Chengjun Goes to Shaanxi to Establish Administrative Office to Supervise the Suppression of Remaining Bandits 24

He Said Before Leaving That the Military Can Be Concluded Within Three Weeks

(Hankou) He Chengjun and his entourage arrived at the Dazhimen Station on the 26th at 0:45 a.m., boarded the No. 55 special train and left Hankou for the north. Those who saw him off included Xu Yuanquan, Chen Xizeng, Ye Peng, Yang Kuiyi, etc., and more than a hundred representatives from various agencies and groups. He told reporters at the station that this trip to Shaanxi to supervise the suppression of the remaining bandits can be concluded within three weeks, and he will return to Hankou immediately. The army commanders left in Hankou will return to their original defenses within a day or two to handle Qingxiang and assist in post-disaster recovery. Because it was late at night, he asked the people who sent him off to return early. It was heard that Xu Chengxi had been appointed as the Chief of Staff of the Xi'an Administrative Office, and 80,000 yuan had been remitted in advance for the Headquarters to reward the Shaanxi army and various units pursuing bandits. (26th Dispatch)

(Hankou) He Chengjun went north by special train at 12:00 p.m. on the 25th, passing through Zheng to Xi'an, to set up an administrative office to pursue and suppress the Xu bandits. He will return to Hankou in about two weeks. (25th Dispatch)

(Hankou) He Chengjun told reporters from the Central News Agency that Yu (He is calling himself) is still awaiting treatment because his hemorrhoids have not healed. Dr. Lu will accompany him to Xi'an. The Xu bandits are now fleeing into the deep mountains in Chenggu and other areas on the Sichuan-Shaanxi border. Our army has heavily surrounded them. Chairman Yang (Hucheng) has taken a plane to Hanzhong to command and supervise the suppression of the remaining bandits. They lack salt and rice, and their clothes cannot cover their bodies, but they can be cleared in a short period of time. This time, he was ordered to go to Xi'an to organize an administrative office to supervise the pursuit and suppression, which is the intention of the Commander-in-Chief to eliminate evil, and he will definitely eliminate the remaining bandits as soon as possible, so that there will be no possibility of revival. After the deployment in Shaanxi is proper, he will return to Hankou in two weeks. As for the limited number of remnants of He bandits fleeing to the Sichuan border, the Headquarters has ordered Wang Lingji and other units to intercept them, and they can be cleared within a month. Yu has not heard anything about the reorganization of the Hubei Provincial Government in Beijing. (25th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Hankou) He Chengjun convened a speech to the section chiefs and above of his command at the Headquarters at 4:00 p.m. on the 25th, urging them to be diligent and public-minded, eliminate the bad habits of inertia and perfunctoriness, and serve the party and the country with conscience during national difficulties, so as to fulfill their national duties. (25th Dispatch)

(Hankou) Jiang paid great attention to national military education. Commentary

Future Actions of Japanese Imperialism Towards China 28

Amidst the Sino-Soviet resumption of diplomatic relations, the situation in Rehe suddenly became tense. What steps will Japanese imperialism take in its future aggression against China?

Generally speaking, all international developments are driven by economic relations, as we have repeatedly stated. The past failures of the authorities in the Northeast stemmed from fiercely competing with the South Manchuria Railway and Dalian Port economically while failing to establish adequate military defenses. After the September 18th Incident, they still regarded it as an accidental event, unaware that it was the inevitable result of economic struggle. They withdrew troops and lost the three provinces. Learning from past mistakes, we believe that Japanese imperialism's future actions will undoubtedly be based on economic relations.

As a result of the development of industrial capital and the expansion of production, Japanese imperialism found that its original colonies were increasingly insufficient to meet its needs for raw materials and the sale of surplus goods. It had to seek to seize the three northeastern provinces as its new colonies. The usual steps for seizing colonies begin with sweet words and enticements, persuading ignorant leaders to sign various treaties to encompass the region's main economic interests. When sweet words and enticements are insufficient and the economic interests obtained by fraud cannot be fully developed and protected, they inevitably resort to military struggle. Since the global panic, international tariffs have increased, and the disease of overproduction has worsened. This innately deficient Japan has seen a sharp increase in unemployment and a sharp decline in cash. The national economy and state finances are in a state of utter destitution. The annexation of the three northeastern provinces had already become an urgent plan with no other options. At that time, the vigorous advancement of railway construction and the Huludao port construction work by the authorities in the Northeast posed a significant threat to the Japanese, which ultimately led to the September 18th Incident. We do not wish to dwell on the misfortunes of the past. The reason for repeatedly stating this is only to prevent the people of our country from rashly regarding simple economic resistance against Japan as sufficient and to realize that economic resistance must be backed by military force.

Economic struggles inevitably lead to military plunder, as evidenced by the Shanghai Incident. After the September 18th Incident, the boycott of Japanese goods was most intense in the Yangtze River basin. Shanghai, as the gateway to the Yangtze River, became the center of the boycott movement due to its geographical location. Precisely because it was the center of the boycott movement, the January 28th Incident occurred. "The use of force against Shanghai was to sweep away the high tide of boycotting Japanese goods in the Yangtze River." This is what the Japanese openly declared to the world.

Looking at the future based on the past, the urgency of the Japanese's future actions against China must depend on the progress or decline of its domestic economic situation. If we have the determination and preparation to resist Japan by force, then economic struggle is a necessary and inevitable means. If we do not have the determination and preparation to resist Japan by force, then we should not feed the enemy with food and drink from afar and serve this new master of the East Asian continent with servile and obsequious behavior. If we still indulge in empty talk of economic resistance, taking pride in the enemy's economic and social turmoil, then we must know that on the eve of the complete overthrow of Japanese imperialism, it will still launch a fierce attack on China, betting everything in a last-ditch struggle. The day we are complacent may be the time when disaster strikes.

Observing from the historical trajectory, the demise of imperialism is not far off, and Japan will hardly be an exception. Japan's use of force in Manchuria was a desperate measure when it was at its wit's end, like digging a well when thirsty. Its inability to save its current system from crisis is already clearly revealed. From now on, as the domestic crisis intensifies, the aggression against our country will inevitably become increasingly intense. The management of the three northeastern provinces cannot be effective in a short period of time, and the activities of the volunteer army have already led to a sharp decline in agricultural production and economic chaos. It will inevitably vent its anger elsewhere and take military action against Rehe and Tianjin, which is almost expected. Given the vastness of the Chinese nation and the historical animosity between the Chinese and Japanese nations, the people of our country, as long as they have a breath, will never accept being led to surrender to the enemy. Therefore, the struggle between China and Japan will inevitably become increasingly expanded and increasingly fierce, which is a matter of course.

Here, we must solemnly inform the people of our country that the intensification of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China is the inevitable result of the development of its domestic capitalism and is not due to the ambitions of a few politicians and warlords. If we still hope for its awareness and expect its retreat, we will continue the mistakes of the past and bring even more grief to the future. Our only way out is to prepare for sacrifice, actively struggle, and definitely not dream of any peaceful solutions.

Recently, the railway has reorganized its debts and effectively implemented responsible transportation. As a result, the operating income in November and December has surged, breaking the new record unseen in more than ten years. The stock market of the railway has soared accordingly. (25th Special Dispatch)

Anti-Japanese Incidents Among Taiwanese People 38

The First Batch of Sixty People Deemed Guilty and Sent to Court

Five People Tragically Suffered Private Torture, Burning of Corpses, and Destruction of Evidence

China United Press, Taipei, 25th - The 4.7 million Taiwanese people have fiercely resisted Japan ever since the Qing government ceded Taiwan to Japan after the First Sino-Japanese War. In the past 38 years, there have been more than 30 revolutions, and approximately 200,000 Taiwanese people have been massacred by the Japanese army. Recently, due to being isolated by the surrounding seas and with no way to receive weapons, they have changed their military resistance to resisting through strikes and various civilized means using the power of national unity. After the Wanbaoshan Incident last year, the anti-Japanese situation suddenly became tense. The Japanese military police then imposed great oppression, so many anti-Japanese fighters fled to southern Fujian and Shanghai, gathering overseas Chinese and students to organize groups to respond to anti-Japanese resistance with their comrades on the island. This was especially intense after the September 18th Incident. At the time of the January 28th Incident, more than 500 people were arrested for anti-Japanese activities in Taiwan, and more than 100 people were arrested from various parts of China (Shanghai, Xiamen, Zhangzhou, etc.) and escorted back to Taiwan. Five people were beaten to death in prison, including two people from Zhushan, Mr. Chen and others, who were moved to Taichung Hospital in late November last year and died in less than two days. More than 30 soldiers and police guarded the hospital, not allowing idlers to enter the hospital. The Japanese police secretly summoned their families to the hospital, threatening them with guns and swords to sign their names, allowing the cremation of the corpses, and prohibiting them from talking about the truth of their wrongful deaths. The reason why the Japanese police cremated them immediately was to prevent people from all walks of life from demanding an autopsy to determine the cause of death. Although the police department lifted the ban on reporting on the anti-Japanese case of the Taiwanese people yesterday, the content was limited to police announcements, and newspapers were not allowed to publish anything else, in an attempt to obscure the truth. Therefore, very few Taiwanese people know the truth. Yesterday, it was decided that the first batch of 60 people were guilty and sent to court. The rest are still in prison, and it is not known whether they are guilty or not. It is heard that among those arrested in China, some were handed over to the Japanese police by the Chinese police. Because the Japanese police used the name of communist party members to coerce our country's police, our country's police, not knowing the truth, believed them to be reactionaries and agreed to hand them over. In fact, they are not communists but national heroes who resist Japan. The Taiwanese people hope that our country's military police will be strictly wary of the Japanese's conspiracies.

Japanese Army to Undergo Major Reforms Next Year 39

Dentsu, Tokyo, 25th - In view of the domestic and foreign situation and the course of the Manchurian and Shanghai incidents, the Japanese army has decided to implement a major improvement in military preparations next year and is currently preparing for it. At the same time, it is necessary to completely refresh the military appearance. Therefore, the change on April 20th next year will implement the third reorganization of officers, which is wider in scope than the administrative reorganizations of Taisho 11th and 14th years. It seems to focus on the lieutenant colonel level and does not extend to the second lieutenant level. Also, the reorganization of the army factories seems to be suspended. At the same time, the 17 divisions across the country will be divided into two types, A (excellent) and B (inferior), to implement the scientificization of the army.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 25th - Colonel Yamashita Tomoyuki, the chief of the military affairs section of the Army Ministry's military affairs bureau, will depart from Tokyo Station at 9:00 PM tomorrow, the 26th, to visit Manchuria. The colonel's visit to Manchuria is to investigate the facilities of the Kwantung Army and will inspect the area from Kulunbei'er to Shanhaiguan. He is scheduled to return to Tokyo in mid-January next spring.

Comparison of US and Japanese Naval Budgets 41

Dentsu, Tokyo, 25th - The US Navy's recurring budget for next year is 317,583,591 US dollars, plus 1,332,550 US dollars for permanent and non-fixed expenses, totaling 318,906,141 US dollars, which is equivalent to a huge amount of 637,812,282 Japanese yen when calculated in Japanese currency. This is a difference of 265,204,000 Japanese yen compared to the Japanese Navy's budget of 372,608,000 Japanese yen for next year. The notable items are as follows: (1) The maintenance and repair costs of the air force are 13,435,520 US dollars, plus 5,715,000 US dollars for aircraft and catapults, totaling 19,150,520 US dollars. However, the Japanese air force and aircraft weapon costs are 15,594,000 Japanese yen. If calculated at par, the US Navy is 22,270,740 Japanese yen more. (1) The construction cost of warships is 15,053,000 US dollars, and the construction cost from the Navy's supply fund is 6,000,000 US dollars, totaling 21,063,000 US dollars, while the additional amount for Japanese warship construction is 15,000,000 Japanese yen, which is a huge difference compared to the US. Even if the new warship maintenance cost of 15,195,000 Japanese yen is added, there is still a difference of 11,931,000 Japanese yen. (1) The cost of armored vehicles and ammunition is 3,000,000 US dollars, but the Japanese armament enrichment cost of 21,710,000 Japanese yen is larger. The right is to supplement the Shanghai Incident and other usage and repair costs, so when compared with ordinary times, the United States is larger. (1) The reconstruction cost of the US battleships 組, Mexico, Mississippi, etc., is 14,000,000 US dollars, which is 28,000,000 Japanese yen when calculated at the Japanese par value. Compared with the Japanese warship reconstruction cost of 20,068,800 Japanese yen, it is 7,311,200 Japanese yen more. However, 12 of the 15 US battleships have been retrofitted, so it is an additional cost for the reconstruction of the remaining three. However, Japan is for the entire refurbishment. (1) The construction cost is 24,920,000 US dollars, but the Japanese workshop maintenance cost is only 394,000 Japanese yen, which is a huge difference.

Mutual Assistance, Friendship, and Peace

Plans to Use Radio Broadcasting

To Bless the Nations of the World

Havas, Vatican City, 24th - The Pope addressed the students of the Roman seminary, first thanking them for their praise, and then describing the joys and sorrows of the world in the past year. He cited the greatest suffering as the miserable situation of believers and priests in Spain, Mexico, Russia, and other places. Other suffering includes the increasing disagreement and mutual strife among nations due to the worsening economic panic. The people who work hard should receive just assistance and compassionate sympathy, and the impact of the panic on them is especially severe. As for the joyous events of this year, the most important is the success of the Eucharistic Congress in Dublin, the capital of the Irish Free State. Amidst the various difficulties in the world, the missionary work is gradually expanding, which is gratifying. The Pope is also happy to have installed a radio station, saying that with this radio station, he can bless all countries in the world. The blessings he expresses to all nations are "peace, tranquility, mutual trust, friendship, and mutual assistance." The Pope also wants to hold a commemoration for the 1,900th anniversary of Jesus's death. Threatening to Dissolve the Diet

Therefore, leaders such as Suzuki want to avoid war, manipulating the hardliners in the party, and maintaining the government on the condition that power will be handed over to the Seiyukai after the Diet in the spring. However, Saito, seeing through the internal weaknesses of the Seiyukai, still adheres to a tough policy to deal with the Seiyukai. The two sides are scheming against each other, fighting fiercely in the open and in secret. Because the Genro still maintains the Saito cabinet, if the Seiyukai challenges, dissolving the Diet may be unavoidable.

Pengu Visits the US Ambassador Suddenly to Discuss War Debt Issues 45

Warlike and Oppressive, Japanese People's Suicide Craze 46

Root Cause is the Hard Life

Most are Young People

Tokyo News - According to statistics from the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department's Identification Division, 1,851 Japanese people committed suicide last year (Showa 6), including 1,160 men and 691 women. As of the end of September this year, it has reached 1,846 people. The reasons are suicide pacts (men and women dying together), broken hearts, family discord, difficult life, illness, disappointment, old age pessimism, mental disorder, etc. The root cause is the oppression of life. Secondly, in terms of age, those between 20 and 25 years old are the most numerous. For example, among the 178 suicides (105 men, 73 women) from September 1 this year, 48 were between 21 and 25 years old, followed by 36 between 16 and 20 years old, and 29 between 26 and 30 years old. The above and below are all in the minority. Also, among those who committed suicide between the ages of 16 and 20, women are more than twice as many as men. For example, in September, there were 13 men and 23 women, while in other age groups, women were less than half as many as men. As for the method of suicide, the most recent is using sleeping pills, followed by poisonous gas. According to statistics, 32 people committed suicide with poisonous gas last year, increasing to 75 people as of the end of September this year, followed by jumping off buildings. All of these are new methods that have not been seen in previous years. (World News Agency)

Japanese Ambassador Debuchi Arrives in Washington 48

Northeast Problem and the League of Nations (9) 49

The day before the Administrative Yuan meeting, our country's Chief Representative, Dr. Yen Hui-ching, especially hosted a reception for foreign news reporters at the representative office, explaining China's hopes for the League of Nations. He stated, "Militarism is what we oppose, but when it becomes absolutely necessary, China may also be forced to resort to it." Many newspapers highlighted this statement, as Europeans no longer dare to look down on the Chinese after the 19th Route Army resisted Japan in Shanghai. The gist of the speech was that the Chinese government has no intention of overturning the facts presented in the Lytton Report. The Chinese government may not completely agree with all the points mentioned in the report, but the members of the investigation team were all respected figures of the time, and were mutually agreed upon. The nature of the investigation was purely neutral and impartial. Therefore, challenging the findings of the investigation team, especially when the truth is so clear, is self-evident. The Chinese representatives have come here not to declare that the Chinese government has adopted and insisted on a policy that directly violates the suggestions and advice of the investigation team, and disregards the constraints of the League of Nations and treaty obligations. We are not here to advocate militarism. China has been resisting Japanese aggression bare-handed for more than a year, and is now prepared to persevere to the end. If necessary, in order to seek liberation, we will not hesitate to use all possible militaristic methods. However, the Chinese government deeply abhors militarism, detests war, and longs for peace. The Chinese representatives have come to Geneva to ask the League to grant us peace and justice. In the past fourteen months, although China has suffered extreme pain, it has consistently maintained its faith in the League of Nations, while Japan's acts of aggression have intensified day by day. Its undeclared war has also created many obstacles for the disarmament conference and the future of peace in Europe. We know that what the militarists who control Japan desire is not peace, but war. They do not see the League of Nations' actions as a fair solution, but as an opportunity to delay and obtain a negative guarantee of international non-interference, while still relentlessly advancing the aggressive plans for the undeclared war that began a year ago. The Chinese government's goodwill and loyalty to the League of Nations can help remedy this tragedy, and has done so in the past and will continue to do so in the future. We firmly believe that since we can keep faith with the League of Nations, the member states of the League will also keep faith with China. You are all deeply aware of the obligations stipulated in the various articles of the League of Nations Covenant, whether they have already been invoked by the Chinese government, or have not yet been invoked, but may be forced to be invoked in the future. However, you may not yet fully understand how the main factual assertions in the investigation report relate to these obligations. I venture to summarize them for your reference: First, the investigation team disregarded the reason that "China's current situation is such that it should have its membership in the League of Nations revoked, and all protection clauses in the covenant do not apply to China," considering it inappropriate. The report states that the policy initiated at the Washington Conference in 1922, and included in the Nine-Power Treaty, aimed to give China sufficient time and freedom to devote itself to national construction without being subjected to foreign aggression. This policy is still of concern to the relevant powers and is necessary for maintaining world peace. If you look at the letter from US Secretary of State Stimson to Senator Borah in February of last year, you can see its contents and the special focus is on this point. The investigation team also stated that in the ten years since the Washington Conference, China has made considerable progress in national construction and consolidation. The only threat to the Chinese central government is communism. The government has made great efforts to eradicate communism and has formulated an economic recovery policy, but as a result of Japan's aggressive actions, communist activities have been greatly encouraged and the government's efforts have been thwarted. However, I can tell you that since the report was completed, the Chinese government has had definite success in its anti-communist campaign, achieving great military victories, and various road-building projects, rural projects, credit projects, and other projects to help farmers are being implemented one by one with excellent results. The Chinese government has hired many League of Nations experts to plan and implement this and other construction work. As for the three northeastern provinces, the report clearly points out that they are undeniably and immovably Chinese territory, and 93 percent of their residents are Chinese. Therefore, in many respects, the three northeastern provinces are completely the same as other parts of China, separated only by the Great Wall. Forcing them to separate from other parts of China will create difficulties and endanger peace. The great agricultural development of the three northeastern provinces is also entirely due to the efforts of the Chinese. The relationship between the three northeastern provinces and other parts of China has become increasingly close in the past 25 years, and the Chinese people have become increasingly active in the industrial and commercial development of the area. The three northeastern provinces are China's treasury, an outlet for the surplus population of neighboring provinces, and China's first line of defense. At the same time, the report also states that the three northeastern provinces are not suitable for Japanese immigration. Japan's economic interests in Manchuria are secondary to Japan's interests in the entire Chinese market, or in India and the United States. Japan's treaty rights in Manchuria are sometimes questionable, and Japan often interprets these rights in a one-sided and provocative manner. The investigation team stated that Japan's position in Manchuria was obtained through two wars. In fact, in addition to two wars, there was also the threat of a third war, namely the Twenty-One Demands and the ultimatum of 1915. The rights obtained by Japan through these methods have greatly constrained China in exercising its national sovereignty. Therefore, if this position is not agreed upon, willing, or accepted by both parties, conflict is almost inevitable. The report also stated that there was no so-called independence movement before the Japanese army invaded Manchuria. The planning, organization, and establishment of "Manchukuo" were all carried out by Japanese officials under the orders of the Japanese military, and all sovereignty was in the hands of the Japanese authorities, which was deeply hated by the Chinese residents. If we were to tolerate and recognize it, it would be inconsistent with existing treaty obligations. The report also stated that the Sino-Japanese dispute arose from the premeditated acts of aggression by the Japanese army. The Chinese authorities made every effort to avoid any provocative actions, and the peaceful methods of resolving Sino-Japanese pending issues had not been exhausted. The report also stated that as a result of Japan's acts of aggression, bandits were rampant throughout the three northeastern provinces, and various illegal incidents occurred one after another, unprecedented in history. Organized warfare is taking place everywhere, and the suffering of the people is indescribable. Sino-Japanese relations are in a state of virtual war, and the future is full of thorns. Finally, the report also made a careful suggestion about the Japanese army openly planning this act of aggression under the leadership of the Minister of the Army, and advocating direct action in newspapers. More than a year has passed since Japan began its aggression plan. The Chinese government has consistently submitted the entire case to the League of Nations for resolution with a calm and upright attitude. The Chinese government's accusations against the Japanese army's acts of violence and political conspiracies have been fully proven by the investigation team. Therefore, it is time for China and the world to hope that the League of Nations will take swift and decisive steps to resolve the issue. We firmly believe that Japan's delaying tactics to implement its sinister plan to use force or political conspiracies to exacerbate the situation should no longer be tolerated by us. The League of Nations, the world peace organization in Geneva, will finally show the world that what the League of Nations represents is fairness and justice, and that it has the courage to decide on a solution to the dispute and implement this decision.

Also, the night before the meeting, the League of Nations Broadcasting Station invited Sir Lytton, the head of the investigation team, to speak, and he made every effort to refute Japan's comments after the report was released. Also, the Pathé company invited Representative Gu to speak about Sino-Japanese relations in a sound film. These two actions have attracted the most attention from the public.

According to general observations, Matsuoka's attendance at the League of Nations shows that Japan has implemented military diplomacy. Matsuoka openly stated when hosting foreign news reporters that "Militarism is sometimes better than diplomatic policies. Therefore, we hope that the League of Nations can take positive measures to resolve the Northeast issue. It is like quenching thirst with plums, and the longer the time, the weaker the Volunteer Army's power in the Northeast. It is essential to seek solutions from within. It is absolutely impossible to rely entirely on diplomacy. In addition to supporting the Volunteer Army to continue fighting and intensifying economic self-defense by boycotting Japanese goods, we must also restore diplomatic relations with Russia as soon as possible and arm the whole country."

Matsuoka's speech is forceful and unreasonable, not worth laughing at, but it can be used for our reference. If there is anything to correct in his attacks on us, we will correct it; if there is nothing, we will encourage ourselves. Therefore, it is attached as an appendix.

Japanese Left-Leaning Groups 50

Japanese left-leaning groups, in theory, range from Marxism to anarchism. From the perspective of actual action, they should be more radical than the Social Democratic Party. In other words, their ideal future is socialism, and their reform proposals, whether legal or illegal, aim to break the status quo and establish a new society, without any suspicion of colluding with the military. Only then can they be called left-leaning groups. However, since 1925, Japanese proletarian political parties have sprung up like mushrooms after rain, sprouting everywhere. Their content is not very solid, and the split movement is quite obvious. Therefore, at the beginning of the implementation of general elections, there were only eight members of parliament. Since the sudden rise of militarism and the universalization of fascist national states last year, the various factions of the proletarian political parties have been restricted to illegal underground movements on the left and threatened by fascist violence on the right, and have had to tend towards further division. Therefore, the proletarian party's power in the current parliament is very weak. Out of 466 seats, the Social Democratic Party only has Isoo Abe, Genjiro Sugiyama, and Kanichiro Eda, a total of three members. Yojiro Matsutani, who broke away from the Social Democratic Party and established another faction, has one member. In addition, Shiro Koike, a member of the National Socialist Party who is flying the banner of the proletarian party but secretly approaching the military, has one member. In total, there are only five seats. If the National Socialist Party is excluded, there are only four proletarian party members. If they cannot get the assistance of the National Alliance, their proposals and speeches have no real status. From this, it can be seen that the connection between parliamentary struggle and the left-leaning movement is very shallow. The election of members of the Japanese House of Representatives requires an election campaign fund of no less than 200,000 yen. How can the representatives of the proletariat afford it (?) However, in this time of storms and fundamental shaking of parliamentary politics, it is a strange sight that believers in socialism can actually serve as a embellishment in the parliament surrounded by militarism, expressing another meaning.

The various factions of the proletarian party's legal movement are originally extremely complex (at the beginning of the formation of the party, there were more than fifteen factions). However, after many reshuffles, there is only the Social Democratic Party (formed by the merger of the Social Democratic Party and the Masses Party). Its political program includes: 1. Fighting to protect the lives of workers, peasants, and the general working masses; 2. Overthrowing capitalism and promoting the management of non-productive and financial institutions by the state. Workers must ensure the productive self-sufficiency of labor, establish a labor system that ensures the lives of producers, and complete social insurance; 3. National land ownership and establishment of a land system that ensures cultivation rights, (autonomous) cooperation in agricultural management, mechanization of agricultural production, and state control of important agricultural products; 4. Construction of economic conferences, establishment of a publicly funded education system for the children of working people, and public management of housing and hospitals; 5. Integration of industry and agriculture and balancing of urban and rural areas; 6. Equality of world nations and construction of world peace.

The total number of members of the Social Democratic Party is about 120,000, and the number of workers and peasants it can influence is estimated to be around 250,000. Urban workers are facing the threat of unemployment due to the excessive panic in the market and the implementation of rationalization, which has led to shorter working hours and lower wages. As a result, the social situation is deteriorating. Last year alone, there were as many as 2,456 strike incidents, more than twice as many as in 1926. This year, there have been nearly 2,000 strike incidents up to November, two and a half times more than in 1929. This kind of movement cannot be guided by the Masses Party. In the mass movement, there is also another kind of illegal organization secretly active.

What is this illegal organization? (?) The monster that lingers in Europe has moved to Japan in East Asia. It is the Communist Party. The party has been a secret organization from the beginning, with a small number of members and mostly intellectuals. Its strength was originally very weak. Although it had agile activities in various public organizations, after the two major arrests on March 15, 1928, and April 16, 1929, the number of people arrested exceeded 1,000, and most of the important figures were imprisoned. The guidance of the movement was completely stopped. With the government's severe crackdown and the extreme oppression of right-wing groups, the Communist Party in Japan had to enter an underground movement state. But as far as we know, the details are as follows:

1. The labor movement influenced by the Communist Party is the left-wing masses in the National Labor Union Federation (Japan), with a number of about less than 30,000.

2. The Communist Party has farmer committee activities in the National Farmers Union (Japan). It has cultivated considerable power among tenant farmers. Every time there is a struggle with landlords, farmer committee members are involved (the number of people influenced is no less than 50,000).

3. In the army and in right-wing groups, there are Communist Party groups, and they use the weapons of right-wing groups to carry out some of their violent plans. For example, in the robbery case of the Kawasaki 100th Bank Omori Branch, the Communist Party possessed more than 100 pistols (obtained through right-wing groups).

4. The propaganda publications include [Red Flag] (monthly), but it is extremely difficult to publish. The publications led by it include "International" (monthly), which specializes in introducing the international situation of the Communist Party, "Industrial Labor Communication" (ten-day publication), which specializes in recording the situation of the workers' and peasants' movement, and sells quite well, "Our Science" (monthly), which explains the current situation from the perspective of Marxism-Leninism, and "Proletarian Literature" (monthly), which is a purely public publication, but its sharpness is no less than that of secret publications, so it is often banned from publication. However, the stricter the ban, the faster the sales.

Under this severe oppression, because there are too many social contradictions and general living is extremely difficult, even severe penalties cannot stop the "reddening" of general thought, and left-leaning publications are selling extremely fast. Even judicial dignity has invaded "reddening." From this, it can be seen that the social problems in Japan are serious. Even if it exerts its strength to invade, it is difficult to suppress the progress of the revolutionary movement. (Tokyo, December 19)
