Unfortunate Incident Before Christmas: American Newspaper Reporter Gray Commits Suicide 99

Body Found in the Alley of the National City Bank

It is Still Unclear Whether He Jumped from the Building or Fell by Mistake

The Letter He Left Behind Suggests He Committed Suicide

Gray Has a Long History in Journalism

The Shanghai Times reported that the body of a Westerner was suddenly found in the alley in the southwest corner of the National City Bank on the Fourth Avenue yesterday morning (the 24th). It was learned that he was Gray, a veteran of the newspaper industry, who had been in Shanghai for six months and resided in the National City Bank. Later, they went to Gray's residence on the fourth floor of the bank and found that everything was in order, with no signs of disorder. There were two letters left on the table, one addressed to the U.S. Consulate General and one addressed to the National City Bank Boarding Committee, both typewritten. The letter to the U.S. Consulate General reportedly mentioned the disposition of the estate. The circumstances suggest that he committed suicide. The reason for his suicide and the truth behind it will probably be revealed when the U.S. Procuratorate opens the trial on the 28th. The deceased went to Honolulu twenty years ago and served as a telegraph editor for the Honolulu Broad Knowledge Newspaper. Later, he went to Hilo Island to found the Maiyi News, serving as editor and publisher. He sold it just a year ago and went to Manila to join the Manila Newspaper, but soon came to Shanghai as a semi-retired resident, residing at the National City Bank for six months. He had been suffering from heart disease for some time and his eyesight was also declining. It is not known why he suddenly became tired of the world. Whether he jumped from the building and committed suicide or fell by mistake is still unclear. However, the police and U.S. authorities believe it was suicide based on his letter. After the discovery yesterday morning, they immediately reported it to the U.S. authorities. U.S. Prosecutor Salede, Judge Creswell, and Coroner Bode went to the scene of the incident.

After examining the body and asking a few questions, they ordered it to be transported to the International Funeral Home for burial.

The Superintendent of the Second Branch Prison Is Reported for Inflating the Price of Prison Rations 100

The Price of Food Rice Exceeds the Market Price by More Than Ten Yuan per Dan

President Shen Believes There Is Obvious Inflation

There Are Also Suspicious Alterations in the Rice Shop's Ledgers

The Branch Superintendent Was Temporarily Detained After Being Interrogated

Since the accounting affairs of the Shanghai First Special District Local Court were merged with those of the Second Branch Court of the Jiangsu Higher Court under the order of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, all financial revenues and expenditures have been handled by the Second Branch Court. President Shen Jiayi of the court has a reputation for being energetic and capable in the judicial field. Now, he must personally audit the entry and exit of various funds to determine approval or rejection. A few days ago, Warden Lu of the Second Branch Prison of Jiangsu applied to the court for prison rations, and the price of rice was more than ten yuan higher per dan. President Shen believed that the current market price of white rice was no more than ten yuan per shi, and the warden had obviously inflated the price and was not clean. He immediately sent Warden Lu and the prison's general affairs officer to the Prosecutor's Office of the First Special Court. Chief Prosecutor Wang opened the court for interrogation one evening last Friday and temporarily detained them. The prosecuting prosecutor summoned the owner of a rice shop selling rice to the court for questioning on the afternoon of the day before yesterday (Saturday). The shop's ledger was also brought to the court. Under interrogation, it was found that there were suspicious alterations in the ledger. Therefore, the shop owner was ordered to post bail and await investigation.

Minutes of the Shanghai Citizens' Congress 101

The Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation convened its fourth extraordinary congress yesterday afternoon at 5:00 p.m. More than thirty people attended, including Zhang Yichen, Jiang Junyi, Hu Fengxiang, Cao Zhigong, Cai Qiajun, Liu Zhongying, Xu Yunhui, Ren Nongxuan, and Zhang Xianfang. Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, and Cao Zhigong were elected as the presidium, and Zheng Dongshan was the secretary. (1) Resolution on urging the government to recover lost territory as soon as possible, stop the civil war, unite against aggression, and restore Sino-Russian diplomatic relations. It was resolved to send a telegram to the National Government, drafted by Cao Zhigong. (2) Resolution on aiding the Northeastern Righteous Armies and providing disaster relief to Northeastern refugees. It was resolved to notify the branch associations to forward letters to member stores to donate as much as possible and provide material assistance. (3) Resolution on opposing telephone and tap water price increases. It was resolved to convene various groups to discuss countermeasures. (4) Resolution on boycotting enemy goods and promoting domestic goods. It was resolved: (A) All members should take the lead in promoting them; (B) Notify branch associations to issue certificates of nationality for goods sold by stores; (C) Member stores should seal up Japanese goods and not move them without authorization; (D) Notify branch associations to conduct a strict investigation. If enemy goods are imported, they should be reported to the congress and announced to the public. (5) Resolution on opposing the state monopoly of poisonous substances. It was resolved to search for concrete evidence and request the central government to severely punish them. (6) Amendment of the articles of association. The first, third, fourth, fourteenth, twenty-first, and twenty-eighth articles were discussed in detail and amended and passed. (7) Resolution on strengthening the financial resources of the association. It was resolved to implement Article 28 of the formal charter. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 p.m.

Zhabei Chamber of Commerce Distributes Cotton Clothes 102

More Than 800 Pieces Are Available for Those in Need to Claim from the Association

The Zhabei War Zone Disaster-Stricken Industry and Commerce Federation, due to the sudden Shanghai Incident on January 28, the war-torn people escaped naked under the fire, and none survived. Now, most of the houses have been destroyed by artillery fire, resulting in displacement. At this time of winter, they are suffering from hunger and cold. The sight of sorrow is heart-wrenching. Therefore, the special commissioners have been going to the areas more severely affected by the disaster in recent days to distribute cotton clothes, of which more than 800 pieces have been issued. Petition from the China Commoners' Association 103

Limit the Time to Use Domestically Produced Clothing

Please Establish Women's Uniforms

Cheng Yu, the initiator of the China Commoners' Association, submitted a petition to the Third Plenary Session, requesting that all government officials and people in charge of military and academic circles be required to switch to domestically produced clothing within a limited time, and that a women's uniform style be promulgated and implemented nationwide. The tone was extremely serious. The original manuscript is recorded below: "Because cloth, silk, millet, and soybeans are indispensable to the people every day, and clothing, food, housing, and transportation, the word 'clothing' is the first thing advocated by the Premier. It is regrettable that there is still no practical solution. Looking at the meeting places everywhere, those wearing Western clothes, from head to toe, are all foreign goods. Among those wearing Chinese clothes, very few use completely domestic goods for their outer and inner garments. As for women in the middle and upper classes of society, none seen on the road wear clothes made entirely of domestic goods. This kind of extravagant and luxurious situation is very alarming. At a glance, it can be seen that it is an unorganized country, which does not need to be said by foreigners. Reports state that Japanese goods worth 140 million yuan came to China in September, mainly silk and cotton fabrics, cotton yarn, and rayon. Another report from Japanese merchants states that the shipment of Japanese goods to China has exceeded that of Britain and the United States. In the item of fabrics, Japan accounted for one-third this time, with more than 165,000 pieces. It is also reported that Japanese goods imported to the Yangtze River area last month reached 50,000 to 60,000 tons, with fabrics accounting for the majority. According to Japanese merchants, from December to January, surplus goods worth 50 million yuan will be sold throughout China. The Japanese Qing Shipping Company has already increased the number of ships to transport them. Another report states that more than 800 Russian overseas Chinese in Tianjin are engaged in the cloth industry. Russian standard foreign cloth sells well in provinces, counties, towns, and villages in North China. According to Japanese newspapers, Russia's five-year plan has been completed, and it will dump goods abroad at the lowest prices. Japanese goods will be greatly affected, and even airplanes and cannons cannot reverse the anti-Japanese goods trend. The economic war is most terrifying. Therefore, they are very panicked. However, the Tianjin telegram in the Chinese newspaper stated that Chinese merchants were very happy to see the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia and discussed purchasing Russian goods to replace Japanese goods when the goods arrive in China. Now, I respectfully submit various newspapers and ask you to review them. To resist foreign goods is one thing, and to promote domestic goods is another. To resist foreign goods, we should stop them with strength, and to promote domestic goods, we should proceed with strength. In recent years, our country has not failed to talk about promoting domestic goods, but there is only discussion and no action. The reason is that people's hearts are dead, and there is nothing we can do. Now, I plan to ask the government to implement the important conditions of the Three Principles of the People, starting with the word 'clothing' in the easiest to implement aspects of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. That is, to strictly define the method immediately. All government officials and people in charge of military and academic circles must switch to domestically produced clothing starting from January next year (old-fashioned non-Chinese goods can be worn at home until they are worn out). If it cannot be done in January, then February; if it cannot be done in February, then March. If it cannot be done in March, then they will never change. Then, those in charge will be dismissed or removed from their positions. The momentum must be vigorous and resolutely handled. Government officials and military leaders should set an example and encourage each other at any time. As for the clothing of women in our country today, it is extremely strange. In summer, it cannot cover the body, and in winter, it cannot keep out the cold. At a glance on the road, it can be seen. Therefore, please stipulate a uniform, with lengths and sizes that must not be violated. Any modern women who encounter violence will not be protected by the law. Otherwise, what is the meaning of propriety, justice, integrity, and shame? In short, our country is in a state of backward production today, and the economy has completely collapsed. If we do not make a painful determination and vigorously reform, we will never be able to recover. Look at India. No matter what class of people, they all wear coarse cloth made in their own country and engage in civil movements. Their patriotism is like this. Why are the descendants of our gentry not as good as black people and as foolish as fish? Although the words are sharp, there is no other intention. If you are willing to investigate, China will be fortunate." Cheng Qing lives at No. 21, Xin Chang Li, Xin Zha, Shanghai.

The general distribution office of Shanghai Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company officially opened yesterday. Although it was drizzling, guests arrived in an endless stream from morning till night. YMCA Fundraising Concludes 106

Results Exceed the Planned Goal

The 32nd Shanghai YMCA Fundraising Campaign closed at 8 p.m. on the 24th. The goal of this campaign was 50,000 yuan. In the first three announcements, only half of the goal was achieved. However, in the last three days, the general captain, Mayor Wu, and the deputy general captains, Shi Liangcai and Rong Zongjing, made every effort to call on the captains and members of each team to cooperate and forge ahead, and they jumped to exceed the goal. Among them, the one who made the most effort was the captain of the fourth team, Mr. Wen Hongen, who won the championship. Although the ranks of the teams of Wang Xiaolai, Pan Gongzhan, Li Yuanxin, and Lin Kanghou were different, the scores were very close, and they all exceeded the goal. In this year's extremely panic-stricken economy, and in the autumn of tight year-end funds, the fact that the fundraising campaign of the association achieved such results shows the concern of the social community for the association and the needs of the association for social affairs. The total score of the association is attached as follows: (1) Mr. Wen Hongen, captain of the fourth team, obtained 6,147 points; (2) Mr. Wang Xiaolai, captain of the tenth team, obtained 5,711 points; (3) Mr. Pan Gongzhan, captain of the first team, obtained 5,543 points; (4) Mr. Li Yuanxin, captain of the second team, obtained 5,492 points; (5) Mr. Lin Kanghou, captain of the third team, obtained 5,000 points; (6) Mr. Qian Xinzhi, captain of the seventh team, obtained 4,030 points; (7) Mr. Cao Yunxiang, captain of the eighth team, obtained 3,204 points; (8) Mr. Qin Yuqing, captain of the ninth team, obtained 2,679 points; (9) Mr. Guo Shun, captain of the fifth team, obtained 1,518 points; (10) Mr. Zhong Ketuo, captain of the sixth team, obtained 1,050 points.

Verdict on the Xia Family Guanyin Temple Property Case 108

Unauthorized Disposal is Inappropriate

Failure to Prove Rejection is Upheld

The temple committee of Xia Family Guanyin Temple (now Pengnan Elementary School) on Qiujiang Road West, Zhabei, previously sued Lu Chaomian, a member of the committee, for donating the land base of the Guanyin Temple and the grain certificates to Shanghai College of Law, which caused disputes among other temple directors. Both parties hired lawyers and litigated in the Shanghai District Court for a long time. It is now known that the land base of the temple property was purchased and built by the female nun Gu Quan of the Guanyin Temple from Zhuang Dejiu and Ma Yuanji during the third year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty. Therefore, the name of the grain certificate account in the third year of Guangxu was still Zhuang and Ma, and the grain certificate after the fourth year of Guangxu was changed to Xia Family Guanyin Temple. It is unknown how the land certificate and grain certificate were handed over to Lu Chaoxiu for safekeeping. The female nun died of illness in the nineteenth year of Guangxu, and afterwards, the temple directors entrusted the abbot monk to manage it. However, Shi Mingjing also passed away in the sixth year of the Republic of China, so there is no way to prove it. Therefore, the court's judgment stated that the defendant (referring to Lu Chaoxiu) was unqualified. He privately disposed of public welfare property, which was inappropriate. However, it is impossible to prove whether the plaintiff has the right to sue. Anyone who sues the current occupant for ownership should present reliable evidence to prove the truth of their claim. If the plaintiff cannot provide proper proof, the current state of possession should be maintained and the plaintiff's request should be rejected. The plaintiff in this case cannot prove the source of the land in question and the fact that the certificate was handed over to the defendant, so the plaintiff's lawsuit is without reason, and a judgment is made as the main text. The plaintiff's lawsuit is dismissed, and the litigation costs are borne by the plaintiff. It is also heard that the temple directors said that this temple is the public property of more than 500 households in the area, so they refused to accept the first-instance judgment and will file an appeal.

Ningxing Ship Collides with Wusong Stone Pier in Fog 109

Two Sampans are Damaged at the Same Time

An Old Woman and a Young Girl Fall into the Sea

The Ningbo-class ship Ningxing, which departed from Shanghai at 5:50 p.m. the day before yesterday, arrived at Wusong. At that time, there was a heavy fog. The ship wanted to avoid two importing ships, causing the bow to crash into the stone pier on the east Bund of Songjiang Town. The pier and two sampans of Lu Sanlang parked next to the pier were damaged, and Sanlang's mother (over seventy years old) and Sanlang's niece Jinbao, 20 years old, were knocked into the sea. Fortunately, nearby sampans rescued them. After causing the accident, the Ningxing ship was stuck in the shallows and lost its ability to sail. It quickly hung two red life-saving lights to ask for help. Li Lisheng, the manager of Wusong Maoxing Towing Company, caught sight of it and sent two small towing boats to tow the Ningxing out of danger. At that time, the Zhanghuabang River Management Office also heard the news and rushed a small boat to the scene. After Deputy River Manager verified that the Ningxing ship was not damaged, it was ordered to sail out of port and go straight to Ningbo. However, it was delayed in Songjiang for more than two hours, so it was anchored at eight o'clock.

Unemployed Waiters and Workers of the Hongkou Grand Hotel Appeal 110

The Hongkou Grand Hotel on North Sichuan Road, Shanghai, closed down after the January 28th Incident. The waiters in the hotel department have not been dismissed yet. The hotel originally had more than 100 waiters, each with a cash guarantee. It has been a year since the incident. The workers' representatives have repeatedly asked the capitalists to dismiss the waiters early and return the cash guarantees. The person in charge of the capitalists initially made excuses for sorting out the accounts, then agreed on a date for resuming business, and finally mediated, but there was no sincerity. This caused great dissatisfaction among all the workers. Yesterday, the workers held a meeting and publicly elected representatives to petition the business community, requesting assistance from Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Wang Binyan, and other celebrities, and to uphold justice. The petition representatives also described the various hardships of the workers' environment, pleading that the workers were all working in other places, and the losses were huge and the pain was deep. Moreover, it was in the cold winter, and it was difficult to maintain a livelihood. It is said that Yu Wang and others have agreed to mediate.

The Second Huang Lu Case Ends 111

Yang Fansheng is Acquitted

Li Gengfu, the driver of Yang Fansheng, the owner of the Bao Da Ginseng Firm, was transferred by his employer last winter and jumped from a driver to a comprador of the Tunan steamboat of the China Merchants Bureau. His encounter was a new record in the driver's world. Unexpectedly, the ship's business was sluggish, with accumulated losses, and it was difficult to maintain. He recently resigned and hired a lawyer to sue Yang in the First Special District Court for obstructing his freedom. He said that Yang's sixteen-year-old younger sister, Fazeng, wanted to marry him, but because he was of lowly occupation, Yang's sister asked Yang's mother and Yang to borrow 10,000 yuan from him to obtain the comprador position. Unexpectedly, on the night of February 28 of this year, Yang suddenly ordered two strong men to forcibly take away the photos and love letters given to him by Yang Fazeng. Yang broke his promise, not only refusing to marry his sister to him, but also cutting off the economic assistance for the steamboat comprador position, causing him to be unable to repay his debts. The court had held two hearings, and the defendant Yang Fansheng completely denied the accusations. His lawyer also defended him, saying that the date of the crime alleged by the plaintiff was before the promulgation of the amnesty decree. Even if there were such facts, it would be exempted under the amnesty regulations. The presiding judge announced the verdict in the afternoon the day before yesterday. Neither the plaintiff nor the defendant was present. Judge Liu then acquitted Yang Fansheng. The outside world regards it as the second Huang Lu case, which has now come to an end.

Scrofula Destroyer Sells Well Scrofula, that is, chestnut neck, is the most persistent and difficult to treat disease. If medication is not used carefully, it will not only be a lifelong problem, but also a threat to life. Anquanxing, Weianfang, Haining Road, this city, in view of this, has specially used ancestral secret recipes and precious domestic medicinal materials to chemically synthesize a kind of sheep brand scrofula destroyer, which is divided into external ointment and internal pills. Since its launch, it has only been two months, and I don't know how many people have been cured by the medicine. Therefore, pharmacies in this city have requested the bank to sell it on their behalf. Therefore, the first batch of drugs of the bank has been sold out. Recently, it is processing and manufacturing day and night to meet market needs. It is heard that the external ointment costs 5 yuan per box, and the internal pills cost 3 yuan per box. Wholesale can still be given special discounts, and merchants are recruited to distribute in various ports.

Prerequisite Issues for Improving Rural Education 115

| Letter from Mr. Zhang Tianbai |

(Regarding the discussion of the "Rural Education Problem" raised by Mr. Bao Zuxuan, Mr. Bao's original letter can be found in this column on the 23rd of this month)

The "Rural Education" problem raised by Mr. Bao Yixuan is indeed an important one. However, my attitude towards Mr. Bao's raising of this issue must first be discussed before addressing the nature of the so-called rural problem. Mr. Bao said, "...the notion of breaking the current economic structure is somewhat overly ambitious." Then he said, "...the pressing problems at hand must be resolved immediately." This is the "metaphysical ghost" of Hu Shi's pragmatism speaking through Mr. Bao. In Mr. Bao's view, the pressing problem at hand is not the transformation of China's entire social and economic structure (in fact, for rural areas, it would be better to say "the relationship of land ownership"), but rural education. Here's a good analogy: you go to a working-class district in Shanghai, grab an unemployed worker, and tell him, "Your problem isn't that you're unemployed, don't have a job, and don't have food to eat, but that you haven't received an education. Wait a moment while we promote workers' education." We can guess with our eyes closed what the worker would answer you: "Please stop! Please stop!" Let me tell you honestly, the most urgent problem in rural areas right now isn't education or illiteracy, and it's certainly not, as great men say, promoting "filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, and integrity," but rather the extremely rapid and widespread bankruptcy of rural areas. In other words, the transformation of rural economic relations is the most urgent problem "at hand." As for rural education, it's not the pressing problem of peasants who are starving, becoming thieves, selling their wives and children, and becoming displaced. This is the urgent problem that we, the bookworms sitting in foreign-style houses in concessions, with at least clothes to wear and food to eat, have fantasized about in our minds. What Mr. Bao said puts the cart before the horse, and this is the first point. Mr. Bao said, "...theoretical insights must also take into account reality." Ha! This is the same metaphysical ghost playing tricks again! If you pay a little attention to Chinese newspapers that don't pay much attention to rural issues, you can understand that peasant movements in various provinces, such as the peasants in Yangzhou besieging the county seat, the large-scale riots of peasants in Lingbi County, etc., have already universally and urgently brought rural economic issues, that is, agricultural issues, to the agenda. Mr. Bao still says it's "overly ambitious"! Then our Mr. Bao's "high and far" is truly unfathomable! Mr. Bao also said that it "must take into account reality," meaning that the transformation of the "rural economy" has not yet become a reality, which is even "higher" and "farther"! "Nothing could be added!" This is the second point. We know that "education is a department of the entire political system" (Shen Bao, December 23rd, Current Affairs Commentary), and politics is the superstructure of the social and economic structure. If we only talk about political reform and ignore the transformation of the economic structure, then it is "seeking cooperation with a tiger," and it can also be said that "when the skin is gone, what will the fur attach to?" If we only talk about education and ignore the fundamental problems of politics and the fundamental transformation of the economy, then it is even more "ignoring the root and focusing on the branches"! Even more of a "castle in the air"! Doing the utopian dream of reformism! I am not saying that rural education cannot be done, nor am I saying that we should only pay attention to the transformation of politics and the economy and not pay attention to the issue of "popularizing education," but rather that without fundamental transformation of the economic structure and without considerable clarity in politics, any "popularization of education" or "rural education" is just black characters written on white paper, nothing but deceiving people! Having said this, the article is already quite long, so I will temporarily offer this for public discussion. I will come back another day to discuss the practical issues of "rural education."

How Should I Maintain This Dangerous Family? 116

| Letter from Ms. Chen Xu Jingrong |

My husband is a small businessman, very skilled in commercial knowledge. Although his feelings for me cannot be said to be twelve points good, they are still harmonious. From marriage until now, for several years, our love has never been broken. In the third year after we got married, we separated from the family and established our own household. Later, we had a child who is just three years old this year. However, unfortunately, our family's economic situation was already very difficult, and at this moment, my husband suddenly became unemployed! When the news came, I almost wanted to commit suicide! However, because of my husband, I remained calm. Instead, I constantly thought of various things to say to persuade my husband, giving him spiritual comfort, and even being more considerate of him than before, consulting him with a smile on my face in everything. In this way, unknowingly, another eight months passed, and our daily life almost entirely depended on borrowing money. Later, my husband really had no heart to stay at home "waiting for a rabbit," so he went out to look for work. However, how easy is that? He has been out for four months now and still hasn't made any progress. In those four months, he wrote back four letters home. The tone of the letters was either discouraged and pessimistic, or some veiled allusions to suicide. This situation is really extremely dangerous! Our family really can't be maintained anymore! Sir, how should I deal with this dangerous family? I thought about working as a maid for someone else's family, but in our poor and remote countryside, who would want you? Besides, even if I got a job, what would I do with my three-year-old child? Leave him at home? Then this desolate environment would definitely make my husband even more pessimistic. I absolutely don't want that! Sir, what should I do? Please guide me with your rich experience!

Reply: Ms.'s letter is indeed a tragic and painful cry under the tight pressure of the current society. And this cry is not just the cry of Ms. herself, but the cry of many, many "masses"! From this, we can smell a lot of blood! However, Ms. wants us to think of a way to "guide" her, which is very difficult, because Ms.'s pain is the pain of the "masses." We cannot abandon the "masses" and only think of a "way" for Ms. This, we must ask Ms. to forgive! Here, we can only ask Ms. and your husband to "endure and cope" with it. | Being able to fight against evil forces is good! "Suicide" will not only not solve the problem but will also increase the pain. A smart person would not do it. At present, only fighting forward can break through everything. "Light" will surely come soon!

Sincerely,

Puppet State Deletes and Revises Elementary School Textbooks 127

Deleting and Revising Old Textbooks from the Commercial Press and China Bookstore

Cultural Aggression Subtly Shifts Our Ethnicity

A previous Japanese newspaper report from Harbin stated that the puppet "Manchukuo" has methods such as revising elementary school textbooks and adding Japanese language instruction. The purpose is to use cultural aggression to subtly shift our ethnicity and implement the annexation of our Northeast. The sinister intention is evident. To prove this fact, we have obtained a notice from the Education Department of Fengtian Province of the puppet state to the education bureaus of various counties, stipulating the methods for deleting and revising elementary school textbooks, in order to see a glimpse of the puppet state's elementary education and to alert our education community.

▲ Instruction from the Education Department of Fengtian Province of the Puppet State

For issuing orders: Upon investigation, the school opening dates of this province have been submitted for approval and have been notified. Textbooks should be reviewed and ordered in advance to avoid confusion. However, educational undertakings are related to a century-long plan. All items such as reviewing the academic system, textbooks, and examining teaching materials cannot be done by one province alone to set a trend, nor can they be hastily completed in a short time. We should respectfully wait for a unified overall plan and follow the instructions. Now that the school opening is imminent, we have to formulate temporary measures for relief. This department has invited well-known educators in the province, as well as department staff and school principals, to organize a Textbook Preparation Committee. After repeated discussions, it was decided that the compulsory subjects for junior elementary school should be temporarily: Moral Cultivation, National Language, Arithmetic, Handicraft, Drawing, Singing, and Physical Education, ten subjects. The weekly teaching time and curriculum distribution will remain the same for the time being. Regarding textbooks for moral cultivation, it is proposed to temporarily adopt the New School System National Language textbooks previously published by the China Bookstore. For history and geography, it is proposed to temporarily adopt the new textbooks previously published by the Commercial Press. If the content is inconsistent with the times, it should be slightly deleted and corrected, and a temporary deletion and correction table will be formulated for reference. Most schools have existing copies of these textbooks, and bookstores may also have some old books in stock. Even if it is not easy to collect them all at once, each school or education bureau can temporarily print loose-leaf teaching materials. Otherwise, the teacher can write the textbook on the blackboard during daily class or student self-study, and have the students copy it in regular script. This is also acceptable. The words in the elementary school lessons are not numerous and can be written in a short time, which can achieve the effect of previewing and also the effect of practicing calligraphy. It is twice the result with half the effort and is definitely not difficult. In recent years, students' calligraphy has been careless, and it has become a common practice. It can be used to correct this, which is also an important goal. The remaining textbooks will be temporarily allowed to remain as before. The ten-subject curriculum must not contain any anti-foreign materials, and the directors of the education bureaus and school principals must be responsible for handling this matter, strictly supervising and evaluating, and correcting it at any time. On the one hand, this department will send personnel to review it at any time to promote progress. After the textbooks have been decided and printed, this method will be abolished. The above has been submitted to the provincial government for instructions and approval for handling, etc. In addition to distributing it, this original document is urgently copied and ordered to the bureau and schools to comply with it. This order,

Junior High School Curriculum Standards (11) 128

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Key Operational Items

Ordinarily, history courses in junior high schools are only taught by instructors. Aside from a few exams, students rarely have other assignments. The following briefly lists the important assignments for this course:

(1) Previewing and Reviewing: For each hour of teaching material, specify the pages of the textbook in the previous hour, instructing students to read in advance so that they have a simple concept before listening to the lecture. After the lecture, instruct students to review at any time and ask questions in the classroom at any time.

(2) Classroom Notes: Supplementary teaching materials beyond the textbook, except for those that are particularly important and should be compiled into handouts or copied for students, others can be taken down as notes in the classroom based on what they learn from the lecture, and then organized outside of class. The teacher should check and revise them at appropriate times.

(3) Practice Outlining: The teacher should use outlines to manage the complex and extensive historical facts and help students understand. On the other hand, they can also assign students to create outlines of the clear and easy-to-understand parts of the textbook (i.e., dividing the original text into several sections, each section further divided into subsections).

The ability to grasp the main points and understand the general idea.

(4) Practice Making Historical Maps and Charts: In addition to using historical maps and charts during lectures, the teacher can also guide students in making such maps and charts. Students can practice making simple maps. Explanations of various charts and diagrams can be assigned as extracurricular work for the entire grade or assigned to a few students to create. Furthermore, historical drawings or imaginative drawings can also be based on selected originals, and those skilled in drawing can copy them. (Detailed and useful maps and charts of this kind can be preserved by the school's history display room for permanent use.) Filling in place names on blank historical maps can also be assigned as a collaborative assignment.

(5) Reading Notes, Reports, and Short Essays: The teacher should guide students to read simple reference books to cultivate their self-study habits. Students should be instructed to take notes on what they have read and report in the classroom in turns. In addition, simple Q&A questions or short essays can be assigned to students based on their level.

(6) Practice Making Current Affairs Reports: Important current events can be reported by the teacher as appropriate, and students can also be occasionally assigned to report on domestic and world affairs in the classroom. After the reports, the teacher should make corrections and explanations.

(7) Other: In addition, field trips to historical sites can be organized, and students can create reports based on what they see and hear. During gatherings held by the school on various national memorial days, students can be asked to give speeches or take lecture notes. For major historical events or the anniversaries of historical figures' births, the teacher can initiate special gatherings as appropriate. When the school holds recreational activities, teaching materials can be used to create and perform historical dramas. Such special assignments can be determined by the teacher based on the time and place.

(2) Key Teaching Points

(1) Managing Teaching Materials: Usually, teachers tend to be detailed at the beginning of the teaching materials and brief at the end, which in history courses results in being detailed about ancient history and brief about modern history, or even abandoning the most important modern history due to insufficient time. To avoid this, the teacher should properly manage the entire teaching material, estimate the time, and make an appropriate distribution of emphasis, and create a "Teaching Material Progress" chart.

(2) Supplementary Teaching Materials: In addition to textbooks, teachers should supplement teaching materials at any time, but copying in the classroom should not take up too much class time.

Respectfully Informing the National University and Middle School Students to Implement Education to Save the Country (5) You Huai Gao 129

Chart of Commodity and Money Circulation

Analysis of the National People 130

▲ General Analysis

Political and business circles and recreational circles enjoying upper-class life (property owners): At most 1 million people nationwide, 1,000,000 people

Clerks in the industrial and commercial sectors: At most 15 million people nationwide, 15,000,000 people

University and middle school students: No more than 300,000 people nationwide, 300,000 people

Military personnel: Approximately 2 million people nationwide, 1,000,000 people

Farmers and workers in urgent need of relief: As many as 360 million people nationwide, 360,000,000 people

▲ Special Analysis

Refugees under Japanese iron hooves: Approximately 30 million people, 30,000,000 people

Smokers nationwide: At least several million people, 5,000,000 people

Victims in bandit areas: At least several million people, 5,000,000 people

Impoverished people in various provinces: At least several million people, 5,000,000 people

For special materials, self-compiled supplementary handouts or excerpts from other books should be prepared at any time for application.

(3) Presenting Central Ideas: The teacher should present the central ideas of the history of each period to enlighten students and enable them to achieve the effect of linking teaching materials and seeking systematic concepts.

(4) Making Good Use of Lectures: The history teaching method should be standardized, and in practice, one should adopt a textbook as the standard and lecturing as the center of the teaching method. However, in order to arouse students' interest and attention, lecturing methods should be applied skillfully, such as using storytelling, applying pictures, inserting Q&A, and raising special questions.

(5) Adopting Outlines: Historical facts are complex, and students often struggle to grasp the key points. In order to assist the lecturing method, reveal the system, and enhance students' understanding, the teacher should present the teaching materials in outline form and explain them at any time. It is best to compile and print outlines based on the textbook and necessary supplementary materials to complement the textbook, which can be used as a reference for lectures and as an aid for students' self-study.

(6) Paying Attention to Comparison and Connection: Human evolution is originally continuous, and even historical sites in different places can corroborate each other. Therefore, the teacher should not only pay attention to the comparison and connection between the past and the present, but also seek the comparison and communication between national history and foreign history at any time (comparison, such as the order in which the Chinese and Europeans used the compass; communication, such as the traffic between the Han and Roman empires). Then, although the so-called mixed form is not adopted, the advantages of the mixed teaching method have been adopted.

(7) Guiding the Reading of Reference Books: The teacher must assess the students' level and assign simple reference books for students to read at any time, either for the entire grade to read or for assigned reading in rotation. The teacher must provide full guidance to realize the spirit of "assisted learning."

(8) Paying Attention to the Connection between Current Events and Historical Events: Studying history can reveal the origin of current events, and paying attention to current events can clarify the application of history. Therefore, the teacher should strive to relate to modern society as much as possible within the possible range when discussing historical events. When teaching national history, domestic current events can be reported and explained as appropriate, and when teaching foreign history, international current events can be reported and explained as appropriate. In addition, the teacher should also provide appropriate guidance to students' reading of newspapers and magazines.

(9) Referencing the Common Era: The era names of Chinese emperors changed frequently throughout history, and the standard of historical era names has become a major problem. In order to ensure the accuracy of dates and the connection between Chinese and foreign historical sites, using the Western calendar as the common era is a more convenient method.

(10) Applying Maps, Charts, and Pictures: Historical maps are necessary tools for teaching history, because most historical sites cannot be understood without geographical background. This is especially true when lecturing on the boundaries, wars, and transportation of various times. It is necessary to indicate them on special maps or in ordinary maps. In addition, historical charts, pictures, and ancient object models all have the effect of enhancing students' interest and understanding.

(11) Other: In addition, visiting historical sites can arouse students' imagination of predecessors or historical events. Ancient schools can organize field trips to nearby historical sites during the semester. During the trip, the teacher can explain the stories about the historical sites to the students, or instruct the students to take notes on what they hear and refer to. For those with a deeper level, specific problems can be assigned for them to try to write short essays. There are many methods, which must be adapted by the teacher as needed, and pay attention to experimentation.

(12) Equipment Attached to the History Course: The objects studied by history are extremely broad and closely related to life. Therefore, in order to enable students to have a true understanding, there must be considerable equipment. The school authorities must break the concept that history is a type of literature and science, and regard the history subject equipment and the specimens and instruments of physics, chemistry, physiology, and other subjects as equally important. The school should set up a special history exhibition room or classroom, or at least combine a history and geography classroom with the geography subject. The main equipment for the history subject is: 1. Historical maps (wall charts), 2. Historical charts, 3. Portraits of celebrities and historical pictures, 4. Various ancient objects (such as utensils, ancient steles, sculptures, etc.), 5. Models (such as ancient object models, ancient architectural models). This equipment can be purchased, collected, or self-made, and can be stored or displayed indoors. Not only can it be explained later during teaching, but it can also be used as a help for observation at ordinary times. Even if it is limited to funding, it can first be created in a rudimentary way and then gradually expanded.

Labor (Crafts) 131

First, Goals

(1) To enable students to understand the relationship between labor and life and to cultivate the concept of equality for all occupations.

(2) To enable students to engage in practical operation training to develop their good virtues and habits such as diligence, endurance, precision, and correctness.

(3) To provide them with the necessary craft knowledge and skills for daily life to develop their thinking and ability to design and create.

(4) To cultivate the foundation for engaging in industry.

Second, Time Allocation

First and second academic years: two hours per week. Third academic year: four hours per week.

Third, Teaching Material Outline

(1) First Academic Year

First Semester (Rattan and Bamboo Work or Other Types of Weaving)

(1) Lectures: 1. The meaning and necessity of labor; 2. The theory of rattan and bamboo work or other types of weaving.

(2) Work: 1. Practice weaving with rattan core and rattan skin; 2. Practice making utensils with bamboo strips and bamboo pieces, and weaving with bamboo strips; 3. Practice weaving with straw stalks and making straw ropes and straw utensils; 4. Practice weaving with wheat stalks and making wheat stalk utensils; 5. Practice weaving with ropes and threads, and knotting; 6. Practice wire weaving. Depending on the convenience of obtaining materials in each locality, practice one or two of the above items.

Second Semester (Earthwork)

(1) Lectures: 1. Young people should deeply self-edit with the spirit of popularization; 2. The relationship between kiln goods and cement for food, clothing, housing, and transportation; 3. The influence of Parai products on domestic ceramics; 4. The theory of earthwork.

(2) Work: 1. Practice the clay molding method; 2. Practice the bisque firing and glaze firing methods; 3. Practice the coating and coloring method; 4. Practice the preliminary modeling method; 5. Practice the plaster mold casting and carving methods; 6. Practice cement work as appropriate (but it must be done when there is an opportunity, such as road repair).

(3) Second Academic Year

First Semester (Metalwork)

(1) Lectures: 1. A comparative view of metalwork at home and abroad; 2. General theory of metalworking tools; 3. General theory of metalworking materials.

(2) Work: 1. Practice basic working methods such as cutting, chiseling, and filing; 2. Practice rod connection method; 3. Practice coating method; 4. Practice making simple sheet metal utensils.

Second Semester (Metalwork)

(1) Lectures: 1. Labor and life; 2. Labor and health; 3. Labor and production.

(2) Work: 1. Continue the work from the previous semester; 2. Practice etching; 3. Practice electroplating; 4. Practice making simple wire utensils (but it is not necessary to review those who have already practiced in the first semester of the first academic year); 5. Practice making simple wrought iron utensils; 6. Practice lathe, drilling machine, and planer work as appropriate (if this work can be implemented, the above items can be reduced appropriately, but schools without this equipment may temporarily omit it).

(3) Third Academic Year

First Semester (Woodwork)

(1) Lectures: 1. The concept of occupational equality; 2. The status of modern workers; 3. The shortcomings of Chinese woodenware and their improvement; 4. General theory of woodworking tools; 5. General theory of woodworking materials.

(2) Work: 1. Practice basic working methods such as planing, sawing, drilling, and chiseling; 2. Practice nailing method; 3. Practice joining method; 4. Practice gluing method; 5. Practice painting method; 6. Practice decoration method; 7. Practice drawing method; 8. Practice making simple woodenware

Second Semester (Woodwork)

(1) Lectures: 1. Anecdotes of exemplary figures in the world's engineering community; 2. The unemployed idlers are a great scourge to mankind; 3. The issue of young people entering the workforce.

(2) Work: 1. Continue the work of the previous semester; 2. Practice fret saw method; 3. Practice simple carving method; 4. Practice wood turning (but those without lathe equipment may temporarily omit it).

(1) Key Operational Items

(1) Knowledge Aspect

1. Give lectures on the various values of labor, make it clear that working is a part of life, regardless of status, in order to correct the common misconception of young people who prefer elegance and despise labor.

2. Give lectures on the principles of occupational equality, guide the trend of career choice, and fundamentally break the bad habits of young masters and misses.

3. Study the types, sources, properties, values, uses, and relationship with human life of various materials.

4. Study the structure, use, and repair and maintenance methods of various tools.

5. Study the manufacturing and repair methods of daily necessities.

6. Understand the drawing method of simple working drawings and the application method of scales.

7. Understand the equipment and layout methods of simple machine plants.

8. Describe the general idea of motive power.

9. Study wood drying methods.

10. Describe the general situation of ordinary craft industries.

(2) Skill Aspect

1. Be able to split bamboo and rattan and use cheap materials to make daily necessities.

2. Be able to use various mud works for molding, shaping, modeling, firing, carving, and other works.

3. Be able to use metal materials and use hammers, scissors, files, and other methods to make sheet metal utensils.

4. Be able to forge iron, quench fire, etc., and make simple ironware for daily use.

5. Be able to use simple metalworking machinery

6. Be able to use wood and various auxiliary materials, and use cannons, saws, drills, chisels, and other methods to make simple furniture, stationery, or toys for daily use.

7. Be able to use simple woodworking machinery.

8. Be able to paint utensils.

9. Be able to understand working drawings and make simple utensils according to the drawings to develop students' habits of precision and accuracy.

10. Be able to draw working drawings to show the form and structure of simple utensils

(2) Key Teaching Points

(1) When lecturing on issues, be sure to provide earnest guidance to make students understand the way of being a person in modern times.

(2) When guiding work, promote labor and make students truly receive vocational edification, and do not generate the concept of despising labor towards others.

(3) Basic practice must be emphasized and should be included in a practical teaching material

(4) During practice, pay attention to whether students' use of tools is legal, and do not only pay attention to the results.

(5) For all teaching materials, pay attention to the difficulty of their construction in order to arrange the order.

(6) Teaching materials do not necessarily need to be novel, but the principle is that they conform to the principles of education and are practical.

(7) The preservation and repair of tools is also one of the basic skills in work and should be paid attention to.

(8) When making items, be sure to let them look at the drawings first, or draw the drawings, and manufacture according to the drawings to cultivate students' habits of precision and accuracy.

(9) When selecting and purchasing materials and tools, try to use domestic products as much as possible.

(10) The selection of topics should focus on practicality and also consider aesthetics.

(11) Cost and working time are major issues in crafts, so pay attention not to let students abuse materials and seek to save working time.

(12) It is advisable to lead students to visit factories more often

Resolution of the Student Unrest at Taiyuan First Normal School 132

Students Causing Trouble Expelled and Escorted Back to Their Hometowns

Principal Removed from Office and Personnel Dispatched by the Education Department to Act as Agents

(Taiyuan Correspondence) The once sensational Bingyu student unrest was purely caused by the expulsion of the director of the Provincial First Normal School. The provincial government repeatedly formulated measures and ordered the Education Department to handle it. Only the issue of the principal was not resolved immediately, and internal factions became increasingly intense. Many students from other schools also rose up to support it, which expanded the situation and made it almost unmanageable. The provincial government believed that the actions of all parties exceeded the scope, so it sent personnel to Fenyang to urge Ji Gongquan of the Education Department to return to the province immediately to properly consider measures to rectify the school spirit and uphold discipline. On the 20th, it ordered the Education Department to instruct the school to expel eight students, including Chen Xiyu, Zhang Xingtu, Liu Ying, Yang Yuanrui, Guo Jingyi, Zhang Jinma, Song Xiu, and Li Changgeng. Together with the five students who were expelled for expelling the director, namely Du Lianxiu, Zhang Yaohua, Li Qifeng, Zhang Hanzhang, and Tian Tiande, a total of thirteen students were sent to the Taiyuan Garrison Headquarters by the provincial government order. The students were strictly summoned to the department, and soldiers were dispatched to escort them back to their hometowns and hand them over to the local county government to instruct their parents to take them back on bail and strictly restrain them. Principal Huang Quan was also removed from office for many improper handling issues and replaced by personnel dispatched by the Education Department to strictly reorganize. According to the news, Principal Huang Quan of the First Normal School went to Ping a few days ago. In addition, the inside story of this First Normal School unrest is extremely complicated and has already affected various schools. It is still difficult to predict whether the Bingyuan student unrest can be calmed down from now on. (Evening of December 20)

Jiangsu Education Department Issues a Notice to Elementary Schools in Rural Villages to Allow Agricultural Leave 133

Zhou Fohai, the head of the Jiangsu Education Department, after personally visiting and inspecting education in Jiangbei this time, felt that the opening and holiday dates of elementary schools in rural villages in various counties were not suitable for the actual rural life situation. For example, students mostly need to help their parents with work during the busy farming season and have no time to study. During the winter and summer vacations, they suffer from sitting idle at home and have no books to read, etc., wasting time and losing learning opportunities, resulting in greatly reduced efficiency. It is now heard that the Education Department, in order to adapt to the actual rural life, has specially formulated a standard for the opening and holiday dates of elementary schools in rural villages in accordance with the academic qualifications issued by the Ministry and has issued a notice to the education bureaus of various counties to allow agricultural leave according to the actual situation in the rural villages and reduce the winter and summer vacations. They will draft measures and submit them for approval and instruction, striving to ensure that the annual study time of students in elementary schools in rural villages can meet the limits set by the Ministry of Education. The order and standards are fully recorded as follows:

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department instructed the County Education Bureau: It is found that children in elementary schools in rural villages in various counties mostly need to assist their families in work during the busy farming seasons of silkworm breeding, wheat harvesting, rice transplanting, and rice harvesting and cannot go to school on time. During the stipulated summer and winter vacation periods, the busy farming season has passed, and the children are very idle at home, and they also suffer from the school being on vacation and having no books to read, so that the annual study time at school does not meet the limits set by the Ministry of Education, and the holiday dates often exceed the stipulated restrictions. Such wasted time and abandoned learning reduce efficiency and delay progress, and it is not suitable for the actual rural life, which is very inappropriate. It is found that the academic qualifications issued by this department have the following provisions in the footnotes for elementary schools in rural villages: "The summer vacation dates should be reduced, and silkworm leave, wheat leave, and autumn harvest leave should be granted according to the agricultural situation in each locality." In addition, the county education bureaus should draft change measures and submit them to this department for approval and implementation, which has already been instructed to comply with. Recently, it has been reported that elementary schools in rural villages in various places allow students to be absent from class during the busy farming season, and those who still take summer vacations as scheduled are everywhere. The education bureaus in various places have also witnessed this situation and allowed it to happen without making corrections. They do not implement the provisions of this department to change the holidays, which is a mistake for children and a waste of their studies. This department now aims to focus on children's learning opportunities, improve the efficiency of elementary schools in rural villages, and meet the actual needs of society. It has specially formulated standards for the opening and holiday dates of elementary schools in rural villages in accordance with the academic qualifications issued by the Ministry and will implement them through a notice. All county elementary schools in rural villages that must take busy leave during the busy farming season should first investigate the actual situation in the area by the directors and stipulate the busy leave period according to the standards, and report them to this department for approval and transfer to the schools for compliance before the start of the next semester. If any elementary school principals or teachers disobey orders, take leave on false pretenses, or neglect their duties, they will be severely punished once discovered. It must be known that this is the first point that this department should pay attention to when rectifying elementary schools in rural villages. The directors of the bureaus and the principals and teachers of the affiliated elementary schools should earnestly comply with it and must not neglect it, so as not to incur blame. In addition to separate orders, you must comply with this order.

Standards for the opening and holiday dates of elementary schools in rural villages: (A) Opening dates: (1) First semester: August 1 to January 31 of the following year, 146 days; (2) Second semester: February 1 to July 31, 145 days, 146 days in leap years; (B) Holiday dates: (1) Summer vacation 50 days, July 3 to August 21; (2) New Year's Day 3 days, January 1 to 3; (3) Winter vacation 14 days, January 18 to January 31; (4) Spring break 7 days, April 1 to 7; (5) Memorial holidays: 1. Confucius' birthday memorial day, August 27; 2. National Day memorial day, October 10; 3. Premier's birthday memorial day, November 12; 4. Founding of the Republic of China memorial day, January 1; 5. Premier's death memorial day, March 12; 6. Revolutionary martyrs' memorial day, March 29; 7. Children's Day, April 4; 8. Revolutionary government memorial day, May 5; 9. National Revolutionary Vow Day Memorial Day, July 9; (6) Each school's own school anniversary holiday, no more than two days each year; (7) Various gatherings of each school should be held on Sundays; (8) Each locality may reduce the summer vacation dates or not take the summer vacation according to the agricultural situation, and take silkworm leave, wheat leave, spring plowing, and autumn harvest leave separately, but the total number of holiday dates must not exceed 50 days.
